## Queries List
This page contains all queries.

|            Query            |Platform|Severity|Category|Description|Help|
|-----------------------------|---|---|---|---|---|
|Volume Mounted In Multiple Containers<br/><sup><sub>baa452f0-1f21-4a25-ace5-844e7a5f410d</sub></sup>|DockerCompose|<span style="color:#C00">High</span>|Build Process|Volume mounts should not be shared, which means that 'propagation' should not be set to 'shared', 'rshared', 'slave', or 'rslave'|<a href="https://docs.docker.com/compose/compose-file/compose-file-v3/#volumes">Documentation</a><br/>|

If the docker socket is mounted, it can allow its processes to execute docker commands.|<a href="https://docs.docker.com/compose/compose-file/#volumes">Documentation</a><br/>|
